(*******************************************************************

 Lifting pseudofunctors to monads

 If we have a pseudofunctor from `B‚ÇÅ` to `B‚ÇÇ`, then we can lift it
 to a pseudofunctor from `mnd B‚ÇÅ` to `mnd B‚ÇÇ`.

 Contents
 1. Action on monads
 2. Action on monad morphisms
 3. Action on monad cells
 4. The identitor
 5. The compositor
 6. The pseudofunctor

 *******************************************************************)

(**
 1. Action on monads
 *)
Section PsfunctorOnMonad.
  Context {B‚ÇÅ B‚ÇÇ : bicat}
          (F : psfunctor B‚ÇÅ B‚ÇÇ)
          (m : mnd B‚ÇÅ).

  Let Fm : B‚ÇÇ := F (ob_of_mnd m).
  Let Fe : Fm --> Fm := #F (endo_of_mnd m).
  Let FŒ∑ : id‚ÇÅ Fm ==> Fe := psfunctor_id F _ ‚Ä¢ ##F (unit_of_mnd m).
  Let FŒº : Fe ¬∑ Fe ==> Fe := psfunctor_comp F _ _ ‚Ä¢ ##F (mult_of_mnd m).

  
B‚ÇÅ, B‚ÇÇ: bicat
F: psfunctor B‚ÇÅ B‚ÇÇ
m: mnd B‚ÇÅ
Fm:= F (ob_of_mnd m): B‚ÇÇ
Fe:= # F (endo_of_mnd m): B‚ÇÇ ‚ü¶ Fm, Fm ‚üß
FŒ∑:= psfunctor_id F (ob_of_mnd m)
‚Ä¢ ## F (unit_of_mnd m): id‚ÇÅ Fm ==> Fe
FŒº:= psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m) (endo_of_mnd m)
‚Ä¢ ## F (mult_of_mnd m): Fe ¬∑ Fe ==> Fe
(linvunitor Fe ‚Ä¢ (FŒ∑ ‚ñπ Fe)) ‚Ä¢ FŒº = id‚ÇÇ Fe

‚Ä¢ ## F (mult_of_mnd m): Fe ¬∑ Fe ==> Fe

‚Ä¢ (psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m) (endo_of_mnd m)
   ‚Ä¢ ## F (mult_of_mnd m)) = id‚ÇÇ (# F (endo_of_mnd m))

   ‚Ä¢ ## F (mult_of_mnd m)) =

‚Ä¢ ## F (mult_of_mnd m): Fe ¬∑ Fe ==> Fe
(rassociator (pr12 (make_mnd_data Fm Fe FŒ∑ FŒº))
   (pr2
      (pr1 (make_mnd_data Fm Fe FŒ∑ FŒº),,
       pr12 (make_mnd_data Fm Fe FŒ∑ FŒº)))
   (pr2
      (pr1 (make_mnd_data Fm Fe FŒ∑ FŒº),,
       pr12 (make_mnd_data Fm Fe FŒ∑ FŒº)))
 ‚Ä¢ (pr12 (make_mnd_data Fm Fe FŒ∑ FŒº)
    ‚óÉ pr222 (make_mnd_data Fm Fe FŒ∑ FŒº)))
‚Ä¢ pr222 (make_mnd_data Fm Fe FŒ∑ FŒº) =
(pr222 (make_mnd_data Fm Fe FŒ∑ FŒº)
 ‚ñπ pr12 (make_mnd_data Fm Fe FŒ∑ FŒº))
‚Ä¢ pr222 (make_mnd_data Fm Fe FŒ∑ FŒº)

      
B‚ÇÅ, B‚ÇÇ: bicat
F: psfunctor B‚ÇÅ B‚ÇÇ
m: mnd B‚ÇÅ
Fm:= F (ob_of_mnd m): B‚ÇÇ
Fe:= # F (endo_of_mnd m): B‚ÇÇ ‚ü¶ Fm, Fm ‚üß
FŒ∑:= psfunctor_id F (ob_of_mnd m)
‚Ä¢ ## F (unit_of_mnd m): id‚ÇÅ Fm ==> Fe
FŒº:= psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m) (endo_of_mnd m)
‚Ä¢ ## F (mult_of_mnd m): Fe ¬∑ Fe ==> Fe
(linvunitor (pr12 (make_mnd_data Fm Fe FŒ∑ FŒº))
 ‚Ä¢ (pr122 (make_mnd_data Fm Fe FŒ∑ FŒº)
    ‚ñπ pr12 (make_mnd_data Fm Fe FŒ∑ FŒº)))
‚Ä¢ pr222 (make_mnd_data Fm Fe FŒ∑ FŒº) =
id‚ÇÇ (pr12 (make_mnd_data Fm Fe FŒ∑ FŒº))
 exact psfunctor_on_mnd_left_unit.
      
B‚ÇÅ, B‚ÇÇ: bicat
F: psfunctor B‚ÇÅ B‚ÇÇ
m: mnd B‚ÇÅ
Fm:= F (ob_of_mnd m): B‚ÇÇ
Fe:= # F (endo_of_mnd m): B‚ÇÇ ‚ü¶ Fm, Fm ‚üß
FŒ∑:= psfunctor_id F (ob_of_mnd m)
‚Ä¢ ## F (unit_of_mnd m): id‚ÇÅ Fm ==> Fe
FŒº:= psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m) (endo_of_mnd m)
‚Ä¢ ## F (mult_of_mnd m): Fe ¬∑ Fe ==> Fe
(rinvunitor (pr12 (make_mnd_data Fm Fe FŒ∑ FŒº))
 ‚Ä¢ (pr12 (make_mnd_data Fm Fe FŒ∑ FŒº)
    ‚óÉ pr122 (make_mnd_data Fm Fe FŒ∑ FŒº)))
‚Ä¢ pr222 (make_mnd_data Fm Fe FŒ∑ FŒº) =
id‚ÇÇ (pr12 (make_mnd_data Fm Fe FŒ∑ FŒº))
 exact psfunctor_on_mnd_right_unit.
      
B‚ÇÅ, B‚ÇÇ: bicat
F: psfunctor B‚ÇÅ B‚ÇÇ
m: mnd B‚ÇÅ
Fm:= F (ob_of_mnd m): B‚ÇÇ
Fe:= # F (endo_of_mnd m): B‚ÇÇ ‚ü¶ Fm, Fm ‚üß
FŒ∑:= psfunctor_id F (ob_of_mnd m)
‚Ä¢ ## F (unit_of_mnd m): id‚ÇÅ Fm ==> Fe
FŒº:= psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m) (endo_of_mnd m)
‚Ä¢ ## F (mult_of_mnd m): Fe ¬∑ Fe ==> Fe
(rassociator (pr12 (make_mnd_data Fm Fe FŒ∑ FŒº))
   (pr2
      (pr1 (make_mnd_data Fm Fe FŒ∑ FŒº),,
       pr12 (make_mnd_data Fm Fe FŒ∑ FŒº)))
   (pr2
      (pr1 (make_mnd_data Fm Fe FŒ∑ FŒº),,
       pr12 (make_mnd_data Fm Fe FŒ∑ FŒº)))
 ‚Ä¢ (pr12 (make_mnd_data Fm Fe FŒ∑ FŒº)
    ‚óÉ pr222 (make_mnd_data Fm Fe FŒ∑ FŒº)))
‚Ä¢ pr222 (make_mnd_data Fm Fe FŒ∑ FŒº) =
(pr222 (make_mnd_data Fm Fe FŒ∑ FŒº)
 ‚ñπ pr12 (make_mnd_data Fm Fe FŒ∑ FŒº))
‚Ä¢ pr222 (make_mnd_data Fm Fe FŒ∑ FŒº)
 exact psfunctor_on_mnd_mult_assoc.
  Defined.
End PsfunctorOnMonad.

(**
 2. Action on monad morphisms
 *)
Section PsfunctorOnMonadMor.
  Context {B‚ÇÅ B‚ÇÇ : bicat}
          (F : psfunctor B‚ÇÅ B‚ÇÇ)
          {m‚ÇÅ m‚ÇÇ : mnd B‚ÇÅ}
          (f : m‚ÇÅ --> m‚ÇÇ).

  Let Ff : F (ob_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ) --> F (ob_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ)
    := #F (mor_of_mnd_mor f).
  Let Fe : Ff ¬∑ # F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ) ==> # F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ) ¬∑ Ff
      := psfunctor_comp F _ _
         ‚Ä¢ ##F (mnd_mor_endo f)
         ‚Ä¢ (psfunctor_comp F _ _)^-1.

  
B‚ÇÅ, B‚ÇÇ: bicat
F: psfunctor B‚ÇÅ B‚ÇÇ
m‚ÇÅ, m‚ÇÇ: mnd B‚ÇÅ
f: mnd B‚ÇÅ ‚ü¶ m‚ÇÅ, m‚ÇÇ ‚üß
Ff:= # F (mor_of_mnd_mor f): B‚ÇÇ ‚ü¶ F (ob_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ), F (ob_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ) ‚üß
Fe:= (psfunctor_comp F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
   (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ) ‚Ä¢ ## F (mnd_mor_endo f))
‚Ä¢ (psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ)
     (mor_of_mnd_mor f)) ^-1: Ff ¬∑ # F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ) ==>
# F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ) ¬∑ Ff
linvunitor Ff
‚Ä¢ (unit_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m‚ÇÅ) ‚ñπ Ff) =
(rinvunitor Ff
 ‚Ä¢ (Ff ‚óÉ unit_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m‚ÇÇ))) ‚Ä¢ Fe

  
B‚ÇÅ, B‚ÇÇ: bicat
F: psfunctor B‚ÇÅ B‚ÇÇ
m‚ÇÅ, m‚ÇÇ: mnd B‚ÇÅ
f: mnd B‚ÇÅ ‚ü¶ m‚ÇÅ, m‚ÇÇ ‚üß
Ff:= # F (mor_of_mnd_mor f): B‚ÇÇ ‚ü¶ F (ob_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ), F (ob_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ) ‚üß
Fe:= (psfunctor_comp F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
   (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ) ‚Ä¢ ## F (mnd_mor_endo f))
‚Ä¢ (psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ)
     (mor_of_mnd_mor f)) ^-1: Ff ¬∑ # F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ) ==>
# F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ) ¬∑ Ff
linvunitor Ff
‚Ä¢ (unit_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m‚ÇÅ) ‚ñπ Ff) =
(rinvunitor Ff
 ‚Ä¢ (Ff ‚óÉ unit_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m‚ÇÇ))) ‚Ä¢ Fe

    
B‚ÇÅ, B‚ÇÇ: bicat
F: psfunctor B‚ÇÅ B‚ÇÇ
m‚ÇÅ, m‚ÇÇ: mnd B‚ÇÅ
f: mnd B‚ÇÅ ‚ü¶ m‚ÇÅ, m‚ÇÇ ‚üß
Ff:= # F (mor_of_mnd_mor f): B‚ÇÇ ‚ü¶ F (ob_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ), F (ob_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ) ‚üß
Fe:= (psfunctor_comp F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
   (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ) ‚Ä¢ ## F (mnd_mor_endo f))
‚Ä¢ (psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ)
     (mor_of_mnd_mor f)) ^-1: Ff ¬∑ # F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ) ==>
# F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ) ¬∑ Ff
linvunitor (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f))
‚Ä¢ (unit_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m‚ÇÅ)
   ‚ñπ # F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)) =
(rinvunitor (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f))
 ‚Ä¢ (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
    ‚óÉ unit_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m‚ÇÇ)))
‚Ä¢ ((psfunctor_comp F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
      (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ) ‚Ä¢ ## F (mnd_mor_endo f))
   ‚Ä¢ (psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ)
        (mor_of_mnd_mor f)) ^-1)

    
B‚ÇÅ, B‚ÇÇ: bicat
F: psfunctor B‚ÇÅ B‚ÇÇ
m‚ÇÅ, m‚ÇÇ: mnd B‚ÇÅ
f: mnd B‚ÇÅ ‚ü¶ m‚ÇÅ, m‚ÇÇ ‚üß
Ff:= # F (mor_of_mnd_mor f): B‚ÇÇ ‚ü¶ F (ob_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ), F (ob_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ) ‚üß
Fe:= (psfunctor_comp F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
   (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ) ‚Ä¢ ## F (mnd_mor_endo f))
‚Ä¢ (psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ)
     (mor_of_mnd_mor f)) ^-1: Ff ¬∑ # F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ) ==>
# F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ) ¬∑ Ff
p:= maponpaths
  (Œª z : mor_of_mnd_mor f ==>
         endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ ¬∑ mor_of_mnd_mor f, ## F z)
  (mnd_mor_unit f): (Œª z : mor_of_mnd_mor f ==>
       endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ ¬∑ mor_of_mnd_mor f, ## F z)
  (linvunitor (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
   ‚Ä¢ (unit_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ ‚ñπ mor_of_mnd_mor f)) =
(Œª z : mor_of_mnd_mor f ==>
       endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ ¬∑ mor_of_mnd_mor f, ## F z)
  ((rinvunitor (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
    ‚Ä¢ (mor_of_mnd_mor f ‚óÉ unit_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ))
   ‚Ä¢ mnd_mor_endo f)
linvunitor (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f))
‚Ä¢ (unit_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m‚ÇÅ)
   ‚ñπ # F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)) =
(rinvunitor (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f))
 ‚Ä¢ (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
    ‚óÉ unit_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m‚ÇÇ)))
‚Ä¢ ((psfunctor_comp F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
      (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ) ‚Ä¢ ## F (mnd_mor_endo f))
   ‚Ä¢ (psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ)
        (mor_of_mnd_mor f)) ^-1)

    
B‚ÇÅ, B‚ÇÇ: bicat
F: psfunctor B‚ÇÅ B‚ÇÇ
m‚ÇÅ, m‚ÇÇ: mnd B‚ÇÅ
f: mnd B‚ÇÅ ‚ü¶ m‚ÇÅ, m‚ÇÇ ‚üß
Ff:= # F (mor_of_mnd_mor f): B‚ÇÇ ‚ü¶ F (ob_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ), F (ob_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ) ‚üß
Fe:= (psfunctor_comp F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
   (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ) ‚Ä¢ ## F (mnd_mor_endo f))
‚Ä¢ (psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ)
     (mor_of_mnd_mor f)) ^-1: Ff ¬∑ # F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ) ==>
# F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ) ¬∑ Ff
p:= maponpaths
  (Œª z : mor_of_mnd_mor f ==>
         endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ ¬∑ mor_of_mnd_mor f, ## F z)
  (mnd_mor_unit f): ## F
  (linvunitor (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
   ‚Ä¢ (unit_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ ‚ñπ mor_of_mnd_mor f)) =
## F
  ((rinvunitor (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
    ‚Ä¢ (mor_of_mnd_mor f ‚óÉ unit_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ))
   ‚Ä¢ mnd_mor_endo f)
linvunitor (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f))
‚Ä¢ (unit_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m‚ÇÅ)
   ‚ñπ # F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)) =
(rinvunitor (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f))
 ‚Ä¢ (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
    ‚óÉ unit_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m‚ÇÇ)))
‚Ä¢ ((psfunctor_comp F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
      (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ) ‚Ä¢ ## F (mnd_mor_endo f))
   ‚Ä¢ (psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ)
        (mor_of_mnd_mor f)) ^-1)

    
B‚ÇÅ, B‚ÇÇ: bicat
F: psfunctor B‚ÇÅ B‚ÇÇ
m‚ÇÅ, m‚ÇÇ: mnd B‚ÇÅ
f: mnd B‚ÇÅ ‚ü¶ m‚ÇÅ, m‚ÇÇ ‚üß
Ff:= # F (mor_of_mnd_mor f): B‚ÇÇ ‚ü¶ F (ob_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ), F (ob_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ) ‚üß
Fe:= (psfunctor_comp F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
   (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ) ‚Ä¢ ## F (mnd_mor_endo f))
‚Ä¢ (psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ)
     (mor_of_mnd_mor f)) ^-1: Ff ¬∑ # F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ) ==>
# F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ) ¬∑ Ff
p: ## F (linvunitor (mor_of_mnd_mor f))
‚Ä¢ ## F (unit_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ ‚ñπ mor_of_mnd_mor f) =
(## F (rinvunitor (mor_of_mnd_mor f))
 ‚Ä¢ ## F (mor_of_mnd_mor f ‚óÉ unit_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ))
‚Ä¢ ## F (mnd_mor_endo f)
linvunitor (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f))
‚Ä¢ (unit_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m‚ÇÅ)
   ‚ñπ # F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)) =
(rinvunitor (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f))
 ‚Ä¢ (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
    ‚óÉ unit_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m‚ÇÇ)))
‚Ä¢ ((psfunctor_comp F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
      (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ) ‚Ä¢ ## F (mnd_mor_endo f))
   ‚Ä¢ (psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ)
        (mor_of_mnd_mor f)) ^-1)

    
B‚ÇÅ, B‚ÇÇ: bicat
F: psfunctor B‚ÇÅ B‚ÇÇ
m‚ÇÅ, m‚ÇÇ: mnd B‚ÇÅ
f: mnd B‚ÇÅ ‚ü¶ m‚ÇÅ, m‚ÇÇ ‚üß
Ff:= # F (mor_of_mnd_mor f): B‚ÇÇ ‚ü¶ F (ob_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ), F (ob_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ) ‚üß
Fe:= (psfunctor_comp F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
   (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ) ‚Ä¢ ## F (mnd_mor_endo f))
‚Ä¢ (psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ)
     (mor_of_mnd_mor f)) ^-1: Ff ¬∑ # F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ) ==>
# F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ) ¬∑ Ff
p: ((linvunitor (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f))
  ‚Ä¢ (psfunctor_id F (ob_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ)
     ‚ñπ # F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)))
 ‚Ä¢ psfunctor_comp F (id‚ÇÅ (ob_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ))
     (mor_of_mnd_mor f))
‚Ä¢ ## F (unit_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ ‚ñπ mor_of_mnd_mor f) =
(## F (rinvunitor (mor_of_mnd_mor f))
 ‚Ä¢ ## F (mor_of_mnd_mor f ‚óÉ unit_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ))
‚Ä¢ ## F (mnd_mor_endo f)
linvunitor (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f))
‚Ä¢ (unit_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m‚ÇÅ)
   ‚ñπ # F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)) =
(rinvunitor (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f))
 ‚Ä¢ (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
    ‚óÉ unit_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m‚ÇÇ)))
‚Ä¢ ((psfunctor_comp F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
      (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ) ‚Ä¢ ## F (mnd_mor_endo f))
   ‚Ä¢ (psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ)
        (mor_of_mnd_mor f)) ^-1)

    
B‚ÇÅ, B‚ÇÇ: bicat
F: psfunctor B‚ÇÅ B‚ÇÇ
m‚ÇÅ, m‚ÇÇ: mnd B‚ÇÅ
f: mnd B‚ÇÅ ‚ü¶ m‚ÇÅ, m‚ÇÇ ‚üß
Ff:= # F (mor_of_mnd_mor f): B‚ÇÇ ‚ü¶ F (ob_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ), F (ob_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ) ‚üß
Fe:= (psfunctor_comp F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
   (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ) ‚Ä¢ ## F (mnd_mor_endo f))
‚Ä¢ (psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ)
     (mor_of_mnd_mor f)) ^-1: Ff ¬∑ # F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ) ==>
# F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ) ¬∑ Ff
p: ((linvunitor (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f))
  ‚Ä¢ (psfunctor_id F (ob_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ)
     ‚ñπ # F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)))
 ‚Ä¢ psfunctor_comp F (id‚ÇÅ (ob_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ))
     (mor_of_mnd_mor f))
‚Ä¢ ## F (unit_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ ‚ñπ mor_of_mnd_mor f) =
(((rinvunitor (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f))
   ‚Ä¢ (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
      ‚óÉ psfunctor_id F (ob_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ)))
  ‚Ä¢ psfunctor_comp F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
      (id‚ÇÅ (ob_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ)))
 ‚Ä¢ ## F (mor_of_mnd_mor f ‚óÉ unit_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ))
‚Ä¢ ## F (mnd_mor_endo f)
linvunitor (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f))
‚Ä¢ (unit_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m‚ÇÅ)
   ‚ñπ # F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)) =
(rinvunitor (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f))
 ‚Ä¢ (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
    ‚óÉ unit_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m‚ÇÇ)))
‚Ä¢ ((psfunctor_comp F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
      (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ) ‚Ä¢ ## F (mnd_mor_endo f))
   ‚Ä¢ (psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ)
        (mor_of_mnd_mor f)) ^-1)

    
B‚ÇÅ, B‚ÇÇ: bicat
F: psfunctor B‚ÇÅ B‚ÇÇ
m‚ÇÅ, m‚ÇÇ: mnd B‚ÇÅ
f: mnd B‚ÇÅ ‚ü¶ m‚ÇÅ, m‚ÇÇ ‚üß
Ff:= # F (mor_of_mnd_mor f): B‚ÇÇ ‚ü¶ F (ob_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ), F (ob_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ) ‚üß
Fe:= (psfunctor_comp F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
   (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ) ‚Ä¢ ## F (mnd_mor_endo f))
‚Ä¢ (psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ)
     (mor_of_mnd_mor f)) ^-1: Ff ¬∑ # F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ) ==>
# F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ) ¬∑ Ff
p: linvunitor (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f))
‚Ä¢ ((psfunctor_id F (ob_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ)
    ‚ñπ # F (mor_of_mnd_mor f))
   ‚Ä¢ (psfunctor_comp F (id‚ÇÅ (ob_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ))
        (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
      ‚Ä¢ ## F (unit_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ ‚ñπ mor_of_mnd_mor f))) =
rinvunitor (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f))
‚Ä¢ ((# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
    ‚óÉ psfunctor_id F (ob_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ))
   ‚Ä¢ (psfunctor_comp F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
        (id‚ÇÅ (ob_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ))
      ‚Ä¢ (## F (mor_of_mnd_mor f ‚óÉ unit_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ)
         ‚Ä¢ ## F (mnd_mor_endo f))))
linvunitor (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f))
‚Ä¢ (unit_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m‚ÇÅ)
   ‚ñπ # F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)) =
(rinvunitor (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f))
 ‚Ä¢ (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
    ‚óÉ unit_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m‚ÇÇ)))
‚Ä¢ ((psfunctor_comp F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
      (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ) ‚Ä¢ ## F (mnd_mor_endo f))

   (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ) ‚Ä¢ ## F (mnd_mor_endo f))
‚Ä¢ (psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ)
     (mor_of_mnd_mor f)) ^-1: Ff ¬∑ # F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ) ==>
# F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ) ¬∑ Ff
p: linvunitor (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f))
‚Ä¢ ((psfunctor_id F (ob_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ)
    ‚ñπ # F (mor_of_mnd_mor f))
   ‚Ä¢ ((## F (unit_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ)
       ‚ñπ # F (mor_of_mnd_mor f))
      ‚Ä¢ psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ)
          (mor_of_mnd_mor f))) =
rinvunitor (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f))
‚Ä¢ ((# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
    ‚óÉ psfunctor_id F (ob_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ))
   ‚Ä¢ (psfunctor_comp F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
        (id‚ÇÅ (ob_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ))
      ‚Ä¢ (## F (mor_of_mnd_mor f ‚óÉ unit_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ)
         ‚Ä¢ ## F (mnd_mor_endo f))))
(# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
 ‚óÉ psfunctor_id F (ob_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ))
‚Ä¢ ((# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f) ‚óÉ ## F (unit_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ))
   ‚Ä¢ psfunctor_comp F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
       (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ)) =
(# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
 ‚óÉ psfunctor_id F (ob_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ))
‚Ä¢ ((# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f) ‚óÉ ## F (unit_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ))
   ‚Ä¢ psfunctor_comp F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
       (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ))

      apply idpath.
  Qed.

  
B‚ÇÅ, B‚ÇÇ: bicat
F: psfunctor B‚ÇÅ B‚ÇÇ
m‚ÇÅ, m‚ÇÇ: mnd B‚ÇÅ
f: mnd B‚ÇÅ ‚ü¶ m‚ÇÅ, m‚ÇÇ ‚üß
Ff:= # F (mor_of_mnd_mor f): B‚ÇÇ ‚ü¶ F (ob_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ), F (ob_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ) ‚üß
Fe:= (psfunctor_comp F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
   (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ) ‚Ä¢ ## F (mnd_mor_endo f))
‚Ä¢ (psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ)
     (mor_of_mnd_mor f)) ^-1: Ff ¬∑ # F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ) ==>
# F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ) ¬∑ Ff
((((lassociator Ff (# F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ))
      (# F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ))
    ‚Ä¢ (Fe ‚ñπ # F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ)))
   ‚Ä¢ rassociator (# F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ)) Ff
       (# F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ)))
  ‚Ä¢ (# F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ) ‚óÉ Fe))
 ‚Ä¢ lassociator (# F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ))
     (# F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ)) Ff)
‚Ä¢ (mult_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m‚ÇÅ) ‚ñπ Ff) =
(Ff ‚óÉ mult_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m‚ÇÇ)) ‚Ä¢ Fe

F: psfunctor B‚ÇÅ B‚ÇÇ

f: mnd B‚ÇÅ ‚ü¶ m‚ÇÅ, m‚ÇÇ ‚üß

   (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ) ‚Ä¢ ## F (mnd_mor_endo f))

p:= maponpaths
  (Œª z : mor_of_mnd_mor f
         ¬∑ (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ ¬∑ endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ) ==>
         endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ ¬∑ mor_of_mnd_mor f, ## F z)
  (mnd_mor_mu f): (Œª z : mor_of_mnd_mor f
       ¬∑ (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ ¬∑ endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ) ==>
       endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ ¬∑ mor_of_mnd_mor f, ## F z)
  (((((lassociator (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
         (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ) (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ)
       ‚Ä¢ (mnd_mor_endo f ‚ñπ endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ))
      ‚Ä¢ rassociator (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ)
          (mor_of_mnd_mor f) (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ))
     ‚Ä¢ (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ ‚óÉ mnd_mor_endo f))
    ‚Ä¢ lassociator (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ)
        (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ) (mor_of_mnd_mor f))
   ‚Ä¢ (mult_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ ‚ñπ mor_of_mnd_mor f)) =
(Œª z : mor_of_mnd_mor f
       ¬∑ (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ ¬∑ endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ) ==>
       endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ ¬∑ mor_of_mnd_mor f, ## F z)
  ((mor_of_mnd_mor f ‚óÉ mult_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ)
   ‚Ä¢ mnd_mor_endo f)
((((lassociator (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f))
      (# F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ)) (# F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ))
    ‚Ä¢ (((psfunctor_comp F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
           (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ) ‚Ä¢ ## F (mnd_mor_endo f))
        ‚Ä¢ (psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ)
             (mor_of_mnd_mor f)) ^-1)
       ‚ñπ # F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ)))
   ‚Ä¢ rassociator (# F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ))
       (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)) (# F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ)))
  ‚Ä¢ (# F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ)
     ‚óÉ ((psfunctor_comp F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
           (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ) ‚Ä¢ ## F (mnd_mor_endo f))
        ‚Ä¢ (psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ)
             (mor_of_mnd_mor f)) ^-1)))
 ‚Ä¢ lassociator (# F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ))
     (# F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ)) (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)))
‚Ä¢ ((psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ) (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ)
    ‚Ä¢ ## F (mult_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ)) ‚ñπ # F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)) =

 ‚óÉ (psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ) (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ)

   ‚Ä¢ (psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ)
        (mor_of_mnd_mor f)) ^-1)

        (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ))
   ‚Ä¢ (psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ)
        (mor_of_mnd_mor f ¬∑ endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ)
      ‚Ä¢ (## F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ ‚óÉ mnd_mor_endo f)
         ‚Ä¢ (## F
              (lassociator (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ)
                 (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ) (mor_of_mnd_mor f))

                    (mor_of_mnd_mor f)) ^-1))))) =

  (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)) (# F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ))
‚Ä¢ ((# F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ)
    ‚óÉ psfunctor_comp F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
        (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ))
   ‚Ä¢ ((# F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ) ‚óÉ ## F (mnd_mor_endo f))

               (mor_of_mnd_mor f)) ^-1)

               ‚Ä¢ (## F (mult_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ)

   ‚Ä¢ ## F
       (rassociator (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ)
          (mor_of_mnd_mor f) (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ)))
  ‚Ä¢ ## F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ ‚óÉ mnd_mor_endo f))
 ‚Ä¢ ## F
     (lassociator (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ)
        (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ) (mor_of_mnd_mor f)))
‚Ä¢ ## F (mult_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ ‚ñπ mor_of_mnd_mor f) =
## F (mor_of_mnd_mor f ‚óÉ mult_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ)
‚Ä¢ ## F (mnd_mor_endo f)
lassociator (# F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ))
  (# F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ)) (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f))
‚Ä¢ ((psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ) (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ)
    ‚ñπ # F (mor_of_mnd_mor f))
   ‚Ä¢ (psfunctor_comp F
        (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ ¬∑ endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ)
        (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
      ‚Ä¢ (## F (mult_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ ‚ñπ mor_of_mnd_mor f)
         ‚Ä¢ (psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ)
              (mor_of_mnd_mor f)) ^-1))) = ?b

      apply idpath.

    apply id2_right.

endo_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m‚ÇÅ) ¬∑ ?f

      
B‚ÇÅ, B‚ÇÇ: bicat
F: psfunctor B‚ÇÅ B‚ÇÇ
m‚ÇÅ, m‚ÇÇ: mnd B‚ÇÅ
f: mnd B‚ÇÅ ‚ü¶ m‚ÇÅ, m‚ÇÇ ‚üß
Ff:= # F (mor_of_mnd_mor f): B‚ÇÇ ‚ü¶ F (ob_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ), F (ob_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ) ‚üß
Fe:= (psfunctor_comp F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
   (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ) ‚Ä¢ ## F (mnd_mor_endo f))
‚Ä¢ (psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ)
     (mor_of_mnd_mor f)) ^-1: Ff ¬∑ # F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ) ==>
# F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ) ¬∑ Ff
B‚ÇÇ ‚ü¶ ob_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m‚ÇÅ),
ob_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m‚ÇÇ) ‚üß
 exact Ff.
      
B‚ÇÅ, B‚ÇÇ: bicat
F: psfunctor B‚ÇÅ B‚ÇÇ
m‚ÇÅ, m‚ÇÇ: mnd B‚ÇÅ
f: mnd B‚ÇÅ ‚ü¶ m‚ÇÅ, m‚ÇÇ ‚üß
Ff:= # F (mor_of_mnd_mor f): B‚ÇÇ ‚ü¶ F (ob_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ), F (ob_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ) ‚üß
Fe:= (psfunctor_comp F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
   (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ) ‚Ä¢ ## F (mnd_mor_endo f))
‚Ä¢ (psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ)
     (mor_of_mnd_mor f)) ^-1: Ff ¬∑ # F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ) ==>
# F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ) ¬∑ Ff
Ff ¬∑ endo_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m‚ÇÇ) ==>
endo_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m‚ÇÅ) ¬∑ Ff
 exact Fe.
    
B‚ÇÅ, B‚ÇÇ: bicat
F: psfunctor B‚ÇÅ B‚ÇÇ
m‚ÇÅ, m‚ÇÇ: mnd B‚ÇÅ
f: mnd B‚ÇÅ ‚ü¶ m‚ÇÅ, m‚ÇÇ ‚üß
Ff:= # F (mor_of_mnd_mor f): B‚ÇÇ ‚ü¶ F (ob_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ), F (ob_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ) ‚üß
Fe:= (psfunctor_comp F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
   (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ) ‚Ä¢ ## F (mnd_mor_endo f))
‚Ä¢ (psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ)
     (mor_of_mnd_mor f)) ^-1: Ff ¬∑ # F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ) ==>
# F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ) ¬∑ Ff
mnd_mor_laws (make_mnd_mor_data Ff Fe)
 
B‚ÇÅ, B‚ÇÇ: bicat
F: psfunctor B‚ÇÅ B‚ÇÇ
m‚ÇÅ, m‚ÇÇ: mnd B‚ÇÅ
f: mnd B‚ÇÅ ‚ü¶ m‚ÇÅ, m‚ÇÇ ‚üß
Ff:= # F (mor_of_mnd_mor f): B‚ÇÇ ‚ü¶ F (ob_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ), F (ob_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ) ‚üß
Fe:= (psfunctor_comp F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
   (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ) ‚Ä¢ ## F (mnd_mor_endo f))
‚Ä¢ (psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ)
     (mor_of_mnd_mor f)) ^-1: Ff ¬∑ # F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ) ==>
# F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ) ¬∑ Ff
linvunitor (pr1 (make_mnd_mor_data Ff Fe))
‚Ä¢ (unit_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m‚ÇÅ)
   ‚ñπ pr1 (make_mnd_mor_data Ff Fe)) =
(rinvunitor (pr1 (make_mnd_mor_data Ff Fe))
 ‚Ä¢ (pr1 (make_mnd_mor_data Ff Fe)
    ‚óÉ unit_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m‚ÇÇ)))
‚Ä¢ pr2 (make_mnd_mor_data Ff Fe)
B‚ÇÅ, B‚ÇÇ: bicat
F: psfunctor B‚ÇÅ B‚ÇÇ
m‚ÇÅ, m‚ÇÇ: mnd B‚ÇÅ
f: mnd B‚ÇÅ ‚ü¶ m‚ÇÅ, m‚ÇÇ ‚üß
Ff:= # F (mor_of_mnd_mor f): B‚ÇÇ ‚ü¶ F (ob_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ), F (ob_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ) ‚üß
Fe:= (psfunctor_comp F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
   (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ) ‚Ä¢ ## F (mnd_mor_endo f))
‚Ä¢ (psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ)
     (mor_of_mnd_mor f)) ^-1: Ff ¬∑ # F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ) ==>
# F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ) ¬∑ Ff
((((lassociator (pr1 (make_mnd_mor_data Ff Fe))
      (endo_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m‚ÇÇ))
      (endo_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m‚ÇÇ))
    ‚Ä¢ (pr2 (make_mnd_mor_data Ff Fe)
       ‚ñπ endo_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m‚ÇÇ)))
   ‚Ä¢ rassociator (endo_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m‚ÇÅ))
       (pr1 (make_mnd_mor_data Ff Fe))
       (endo_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m‚ÇÇ)))
  ‚Ä¢ (endo_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m‚ÇÅ)
     ‚óÉ pr2 (make_mnd_mor_data Ff Fe)))
 ‚Ä¢ lassociator (endo_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m‚ÇÅ))
     (endo_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m‚ÇÅ))
     (pr1 (make_mnd_mor_data Ff Fe)))
‚Ä¢ (mult_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m‚ÇÅ)
   ‚ñπ pr1 (make_mnd_mor_data Ff Fe)) =
(pr1 (make_mnd_mor_data Ff Fe)
 ‚óÉ mult_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m‚ÇÇ))
‚Ä¢ pr2 (make_mnd_mor_data Ff Fe)

      
B‚ÇÅ, B‚ÇÇ: bicat
F: psfunctor B‚ÇÅ B‚ÇÇ
m‚ÇÅ, m‚ÇÇ: mnd B‚ÇÅ
f: mnd B‚ÇÅ ‚ü¶ m‚ÇÅ, m‚ÇÇ ‚üß
Ff:= # F (mor_of_mnd_mor f): B‚ÇÇ ‚ü¶ F (ob_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ), F (ob_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ) ‚üß
Fe:= (psfunctor_comp F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
   (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ) ‚Ä¢ ## F (mnd_mor_endo f))
‚Ä¢ (psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ)
     (mor_of_mnd_mor f)) ^-1: Ff ¬∑ # F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ) ==>
# F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ) ¬∑ Ff
linvunitor (pr1 (make_mnd_mor_data Ff Fe))
‚Ä¢ (unit_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m‚ÇÅ)
   ‚ñπ pr1 (make_mnd_mor_data Ff Fe)) =
(rinvunitor (pr1 (make_mnd_mor_data Ff Fe))
 ‚Ä¢ (pr1 (make_mnd_mor_data Ff Fe)
    ‚óÉ unit_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m‚ÇÇ)))
‚Ä¢ pr2 (make_mnd_mor_data Ff Fe)
 exact psfunctor_on_mnd_mor_unit.
      
B‚ÇÅ, B‚ÇÇ: bicat
F: psfunctor B‚ÇÅ B‚ÇÇ
m‚ÇÅ, m‚ÇÇ: mnd B‚ÇÅ
f: mnd B‚ÇÅ ‚ü¶ m‚ÇÅ, m‚ÇÇ ‚üß
Ff:= # F (mor_of_mnd_mor f): B‚ÇÇ ‚ü¶ F (ob_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ), F (ob_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ) ‚üß
Fe:= (psfunctor_comp F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
   (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ) ‚Ä¢ ## F (mnd_mor_endo f))
‚Ä¢ (psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ)
     (mor_of_mnd_mor f)) ^-1: Ff ¬∑ # F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ) ==>
# F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ) ¬∑ Ff
((((lassociator (pr1 (make_mnd_mor_data Ff Fe))
      (endo_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m‚ÇÇ))
      (endo_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m‚ÇÇ))
    ‚Ä¢ (pr2 (make_mnd_mor_data Ff Fe)
       ‚ñπ endo_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m‚ÇÇ)))
   ‚Ä¢ rassociator (endo_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m‚ÇÅ))
       (pr1 (make_mnd_mor_data Ff Fe))
       (endo_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m‚ÇÇ)))
  ‚Ä¢ (endo_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m‚ÇÅ)
     ‚óÉ pr2 (make_mnd_mor_data Ff Fe)))
 ‚Ä¢ lassociator (endo_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m‚ÇÅ))
     (endo_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m‚ÇÅ))
     (pr1 (make_mnd_mor_data Ff Fe)))
‚Ä¢ (mult_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m‚ÇÅ)
   ‚ñπ pr1 (make_mnd_mor_data Ff Fe)) =
(pr1 (make_mnd_mor_data Ff Fe)
 ‚óÉ mult_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m‚ÇÇ))
‚Ä¢ pr2 (make_mnd_mor_data Ff Fe)
 exact psfunctor_on_mnd_mor_mu.
  Defined.
End PsfunctorOnMonadMor.

(**
 3. Action on monad cells
 *)

B‚ÇÅ, B‚ÇÇ: bicat
F: psfunctor B‚ÇÅ B‚ÇÇ
m‚ÇÅ, m‚ÇÇ: mnd B‚ÇÅ
f, g: mnd B‚ÇÅ ‚ü¶ m‚ÇÅ, m‚ÇÇ ‚üß
œÑ: f ==> g
psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F f ==> psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F g


B‚ÇÅ, B‚ÇÇ: bicat
F: psfunctor B‚ÇÅ B‚ÇÇ
m‚ÇÅ, m‚ÇÇ: mnd B‚ÇÅ
f, g: mnd B‚ÇÅ ‚ü¶ m‚ÇÅ, m‚ÇÇ ‚üß
œÑ: f ==> g
psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F f ==> psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F g

  
B‚ÇÅ, B‚ÇÇ: bicat
F: psfunctor B‚ÇÅ B‚ÇÇ
m‚ÇÅ, m‚ÇÇ: mnd B‚ÇÅ
f, g: mnd B‚ÇÅ ‚ü¶ m‚ÇÅ, m‚ÇÇ ‚üß
œÑ: f ==> g
mnd_cell_data (psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F f)
  (psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F g)
B‚ÇÅ, B‚ÇÇ: bicat
F: psfunctor B‚ÇÅ B‚ÇÇ
m‚ÇÅ, m‚ÇÇ: mnd B‚ÇÅ
f, g: mnd B‚ÇÅ ‚ü¶ m‚ÇÅ, m‚ÇÇ ‚üß
œÑ: f ==> g
is_mnd_cell ?œÑ

  
B‚ÇÅ, B‚ÇÇ: bicat
F: psfunctor B‚ÇÅ B‚ÇÇ
m‚ÇÅ, m‚ÇÇ: mnd B‚ÇÅ
f, g: mnd B‚ÇÅ ‚ü¶ m‚ÇÅ, m‚ÇÇ ‚üß
œÑ: f ==> g
mnd_cell_data (psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F f)
  (psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F g)
 exact (##F (cell_of_mnd_cell œÑ)).
  
B‚ÇÅ, B‚ÇÇ: bicat
F: psfunctor B‚ÇÅ B‚ÇÇ
m‚ÇÅ, m‚ÇÇ: mnd B‚ÇÅ
f, g: mnd B‚ÇÅ ‚ü¶ m‚ÇÅ, m‚ÇÇ ‚üß
œÑ: f ==> g
is_mnd_cell (## F (cell_of_mnd_cell œÑ))
 abstract
      (unfold is_mnd_cell ;
       cbn -[psfunctor_comp psfunctor_id] ;
       rewrite !vassocr ;
       rewrite <- psfunctor_rwhisker ;
       rewrite !vassocl ;
       apply maponpaths ;
       rewrite !vassocr ;
       rewrite <- psfunctor_vcomp ;
       rewrite <- (mnd_cell_endo œÑ) ;
       rewrite !psfunctor_vcomp ;
       rewrite !vassocl ;
       apply maponpaths ;
       use vcomp_move_R_pM ; [ is_iso | ] ;
       rewrite !vassocr ;
       use vcomp_move_L_Mp ; [ is_iso | ] ;
       cbn -[psfunctor_comp psfunctor_id] ;
       rewrite psfunctor_lwhisker ;
       apply idpath).
Defined.

(**
 4. The identitor
 *)

B‚ÇÅ, B‚ÇÇ: bicat
F: psfunctor B‚ÇÅ B‚ÇÇ
m: mnd B‚ÇÅ
id‚ÇÅ (psfunctor_on_mnd F m) ==>
psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F (id‚ÇÅ m)


B‚ÇÅ, B‚ÇÇ: bicat
F: psfunctor B‚ÇÅ B‚ÇÇ
m: mnd B‚ÇÅ
id‚ÇÅ (psfunctor_on_mnd F m) ==>
psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F (id‚ÇÅ m)

  
B‚ÇÅ, B‚ÇÇ: bicat
F: psfunctor B‚ÇÅ B‚ÇÇ
m: mnd B‚ÇÅ
mnd_cell_data (id‚ÇÅ (psfunctor_on_mnd F m))
  (psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F (id‚ÇÅ m))
B‚ÇÅ, B‚ÇÇ: bicat
F: psfunctor B‚ÇÅ B‚ÇÇ
m: mnd B‚ÇÅ
is_mnd_cell ?œÑ

  
B‚ÇÅ, B‚ÇÇ: bicat
F: psfunctor B‚ÇÅ B‚ÇÇ
m: mnd B‚ÇÅ
mnd_cell_data (id‚ÇÅ (psfunctor_on_mnd F m))
  (psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F (id‚ÇÅ m))
 
B‚ÇÅ, B‚ÇÇ: bicat
F: psfunctor B‚ÇÅ B‚ÇÇ
m: mnd B‚ÇÅ
mor_of_mnd_mor (id‚ÇÅ (psfunctor_on_mnd F m)) ==>
mor_of_mnd_mor (psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F (id‚ÇÅ m))

    exact (psfunctor_id F _).
  
B‚ÇÅ, B‚ÇÇ: bicat
F: psfunctor B‚ÇÅ B‚ÇÇ
m: mnd B‚ÇÅ
is_mnd_cell
  (psfunctor_id F (ob_of_mnd m)
   :
   mnd_cell_data (id‚ÇÅ (psfunctor_on_mnd F m))
     (psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F (id‚ÇÅ m)))
 abstract
      (unfold is_mnd_cell ;
       cbn -[psfunctor_id psfunctor_comp] ;
       rewrite !vassocl ;
       rewrite !psfunctor_vcomp ;
       rewrite psfunctor_lunitor ;
       rewrite !vassocl ;
       do 3 apply maponpaths ;
       rewrite psfunctor_rinvunitor ;
       rewrite !vassocl ;
       rewrite vcomp_rinv ;
       rewrite id2_right ;
       apply idpath).
Defined.

(**
 5. The compositor
 *)
Section PsfunctorOnMonadComposition.
  Context {B‚ÇÅ B‚ÇÇ : bicat}
          (F : psfunctor B‚ÇÅ B‚ÇÇ)
          {m‚ÇÅ m‚ÇÇ m‚ÇÉ : mnd B‚ÇÅ}
          (f : m‚ÇÅ --> m‚ÇÇ)
          (g : m‚ÇÇ --> m‚ÇÉ).

  
B‚ÇÅ, B‚ÇÇ: bicat
F: psfunctor B‚ÇÅ B‚ÇÇ
m‚ÇÅ, m‚ÇÇ, m‚ÇÉ: mnd B‚ÇÅ
f: mnd B‚ÇÅ ‚ü¶ m‚ÇÅ, m‚ÇÇ ‚üß
g: mnd B‚ÇÅ ‚ü¶ m‚ÇÇ, m‚ÇÉ ‚üß
mnd_mor_endo
  (psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F f ¬∑ psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F g)
‚Ä¢ (endo_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m‚ÇÅ)
   ‚óÉ psfunctor_comp F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
       (mor_of_mnd_mor g)) =
(psfunctor_comp F (pr1 f) (pr1 g)
 ‚ñπ endo_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m‚ÇÉ))
‚Ä¢ mnd_mor_endo (psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F (f ¬∑ g))

  
B‚ÇÅ, B‚ÇÇ: bicat
F: psfunctor B‚ÇÅ B‚ÇÇ
m‚ÇÅ, m‚ÇÇ, m‚ÇÉ: mnd B‚ÇÅ
f: mnd B‚ÇÅ ‚ü¶ m‚ÇÅ, m‚ÇÇ ‚üß
g: mnd B‚ÇÅ ‚ü¶ m‚ÇÇ, m‚ÇÉ ‚üß
mnd_mor_endo
  (psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F f ¬∑ psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F g)
‚Ä¢ (endo_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m‚ÇÅ)
   ‚óÉ psfunctor_comp F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
       (mor_of_mnd_mor g)) =
(psfunctor_comp F (pr1 f) (pr1 g)
 ‚ñπ endo_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m‚ÇÉ))
‚Ä¢ mnd_mor_endo (psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F (f ¬∑ g))

    
B‚ÇÅ, B‚ÇÇ: bicat
F: psfunctor B‚ÇÅ B‚ÇÇ
m‚ÇÅ, m‚ÇÇ, m‚ÇÉ: mnd B‚ÇÅ
f: mnd B‚ÇÅ ‚ü¶ m‚ÇÅ, m‚ÇÇ ‚üß
g: mnd B‚ÇÅ ‚ü¶ m‚ÇÇ, m‚ÇÉ ‚üß
((((rassociator (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f))
      (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor g)) (# F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÉ))
    ‚Ä¢ (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
       ‚óÉ ((psfunctor_comp F (mor_of_mnd_mor g)
             (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÉ) ‚Ä¢ ## F (mnd_mor_endo g))
          ‚Ä¢ (psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ)
               (mor_of_mnd_mor g)) ^-1)))
   ‚Ä¢ lassociator (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f))
       (# F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ)) (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor g)))
  ‚Ä¢ (((psfunctor_comp F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
         (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ) ‚Ä¢ ## F (mnd_mor_endo f))
      ‚Ä¢ (psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ)
           (mor_of_mnd_mor f)) ^-1)
     ‚ñπ # F (mor_of_mnd_mor g)))
 ‚Ä¢ rassociator (# F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ))
     (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)) (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor g)))
‚Ä¢ (# F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ)
   ‚óÉ psfunctor_comp F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
       (mor_of_mnd_mor g)) =
(psfunctor_comp F (pr1 f) (pr1 g)
 ‚ñπ # F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÉ))
‚Ä¢ ((psfunctor_comp F (pr1 f ¬∑ pr1 g) (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÉ)
    ‚Ä¢ ## F
        ((((rassociator (pr1 f) (pr1 g) (pr112 m‚ÇÉ)
            ‚Ä¢ (pr1 f ‚óÉ pr112 g))
           ‚Ä¢ lassociator (pr1 f) (pr112 m‚ÇÇ) (pr1 g))
          ‚Ä¢ (pr112 f ‚ñπ pr1 g))
         ‚Ä¢ rassociator (pr112 m‚ÇÅ) (pr1 f) (pr1 g)))
   ‚Ä¢ (psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ)
        (pr1 f ¬∑ pr1 g)) ^-1)

    
B‚ÇÅ, B‚ÇÇ: bicat
F: psfunctor B‚ÇÅ B‚ÇÇ
m‚ÇÅ, m‚ÇÇ, m‚ÇÉ: mnd B‚ÇÅ
f: mnd B‚ÇÅ ‚ü¶ m‚ÇÅ, m‚ÇÇ ‚üß
g: mnd B‚ÇÅ ‚ü¶ m‚ÇÇ, m‚ÇÉ ‚üß
((((rassociator (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f))
      (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor g)) (# F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÉ))
    ‚Ä¢ (((# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
         ‚óÉ psfunctor_comp F (mor_of_mnd_mor g)
             (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÉ))
        ‚Ä¢ (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
           ‚óÉ ## F (mnd_mor_endo g)))
       ‚Ä¢ (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
          ‚óÉ (psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ)
               (mor_of_mnd_mor g)) ^-1)))
   ‚Ä¢ lassociator (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f))
       (# F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ)) (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor g)))
  ‚Ä¢ (((psfunctor_comp F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
         (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÇ) ‚Ä¢ ## F (mnd_mor_endo f))
      ‚Ä¢ (psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ)
           (mor_of_mnd_mor f)) ^-1)
     ‚ñπ # F (mor_of_mnd_mor g)))
 ‚Ä¢ rassociator (# F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ))
     (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)) (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor g)))
‚Ä¢ (# F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÅ)
   ‚óÉ psfunctor_comp F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
       (mor_of_mnd_mor g)) =
(psfunctor_comp F (pr1 f) (pr1 g)
 ‚ñπ # F (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÉ))
‚Ä¢ ((psfunctor_comp F (pr1 f ¬∑ pr1 g) (endo_of_mnd m‚ÇÉ)
    ‚Ä¢ ## F
        ((((rassociator (pr1 f) (pr1 g) (pr112 m‚ÇÉ)
            ‚Ä¢ (pr1 f ‚óÉ pr112 g))

F: psfunctor B‚ÇÅ B‚ÇÇ
m‚ÇÅ, m‚ÇÇ, m‚ÇÉ: mnd B‚ÇÅ
f: mnd B‚ÇÅ ‚ü¶ m‚ÇÅ, m‚ÇÇ ‚üß
g: mnd B‚ÇÅ ‚ü¶ m‚ÇÇ, m‚ÇÉ ‚üß
psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F f ¬∑ psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F g ==>
psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F (f ¬∑ g)

  
B‚ÇÅ, B‚ÇÇ: bicat
F: psfunctor B‚ÇÅ B‚ÇÇ
m‚ÇÅ, m‚ÇÇ, m‚ÇÉ: mnd B‚ÇÅ
f: mnd B‚ÇÅ ‚ü¶ m‚ÇÅ, m‚ÇÇ ‚üß
g: mnd B‚ÇÅ ‚ü¶ m‚ÇÇ, m‚ÇÉ ‚üß
psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F f ¬∑ psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F g ==>
psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F (f ¬∑ g)

    
B‚ÇÅ, B‚ÇÇ: bicat
F: psfunctor B‚ÇÅ B‚ÇÇ
m‚ÇÅ, m‚ÇÇ, m‚ÇÉ: mnd B‚ÇÅ
f: mnd B‚ÇÅ ‚ü¶ m‚ÇÅ, m‚ÇÇ ‚üß
g: mnd B‚ÇÅ ‚ü¶ m‚ÇÇ, m‚ÇÉ ‚üß
mnd_cell_data
  (psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F f ¬∑ psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F g)
  (psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F (f ¬∑ g))
B‚ÇÅ, B‚ÇÇ: bicat
F: psfunctor B‚ÇÅ B‚ÇÇ
m‚ÇÅ, m‚ÇÇ, m‚ÇÉ: mnd B‚ÇÅ
f: mnd B‚ÇÅ ‚ü¶ m‚ÇÅ, m‚ÇÇ ‚üß
g: mnd B‚ÇÅ ‚ü¶ m‚ÇÇ, m‚ÇÉ ‚üß
is_mnd_cell ?œÑ

    
B‚ÇÅ, B‚ÇÇ: bicat
F: psfunctor B‚ÇÅ B‚ÇÇ
m‚ÇÅ, m‚ÇÇ, m‚ÇÉ: mnd B‚ÇÅ
f: mnd B‚ÇÅ ‚ü¶ m‚ÇÅ, m‚ÇÇ ‚üß
g: mnd B‚ÇÅ ‚ü¶ m‚ÇÇ, m‚ÇÉ ‚üß
mnd_cell_data
  (psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F f ¬∑ psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F g)
  (psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F (f ¬∑ g))
 
B‚ÇÅ, B‚ÇÇ: bicat
F: psfunctor B‚ÇÅ B‚ÇÇ
m‚ÇÅ, m‚ÇÇ, m‚ÇÉ: mnd B‚ÇÅ
f: mnd B‚ÇÅ ‚ü¶ m‚ÇÅ, m‚ÇÇ ‚üß
g: mnd B‚ÇÅ ‚ü¶ m‚ÇÇ, m‚ÇÉ ‚üß
mor_of_mnd_mor
  (psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F f ¬∑ psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F g) ==>
mor_of_mnd_mor (psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F (f ¬∑ g))

      exact (psfunctor_comp F _ _).
    
B‚ÇÅ, B‚ÇÇ: bicat
F: psfunctor B‚ÇÅ B‚ÇÇ
m‚ÇÅ, m‚ÇÇ, m‚ÇÉ: mnd B‚ÇÅ
f: mnd B‚ÇÅ ‚ü¶ m‚ÇÅ, m‚ÇÇ ‚üß
g: mnd B‚ÇÅ ‚ü¶ m‚ÇÇ, m‚ÇÉ ‚üß
is_mnd_cell
  (psfunctor_comp F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
     (mor_of_mnd_mor g)
   :
   mnd_cell_data
     (psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F f
      ¬∑ psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F g)
     (psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F (f ¬∑ g)))
 
B‚ÇÅ, B‚ÇÇ: bicat
F: psfunctor B‚ÇÅ B‚ÇÇ
m‚ÇÅ, m‚ÇÇ, m‚ÇÉ: mnd B‚ÇÅ
f: mnd B‚ÇÅ ‚ü¶ m‚ÇÅ, m‚ÇÇ ‚üß
g: mnd B‚ÇÅ ‚ü¶ m‚ÇÇ, m‚ÇÉ ‚üß
mnd_mor_endo
  (psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F f ¬∑ psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F g)
‚Ä¢ (endo_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m‚ÇÅ)
   ‚óÉ psfunctor_comp F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
       (mor_of_mnd_mor g)) =
(psfunctor_comp F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
   (mor_of_mnd_mor g)
 ‚ñπ endo_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m‚ÇÉ))
‚Ä¢ mnd_mor_endo (psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F (f ¬∑ g))

      exact psfunctor_on_mnd_comp_mor_endo.
  Defined.
End PsfunctorOnMonadComposition.
